SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071278 COCA  A    0  100 A final insult as well as an additional indication of Ishi 's museum-piece status is that after his death the space he lived in was immediately cleared and made ready for the next display : " Gifford ordered the door to the empty room opened , and the Pacific Islands and reinstalled.
